# <a name="obsolete-types-in-the-net-framework"></a><span data-ttu-id="1b42d-104">.NET Framework 中過時的類型</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="1b42d-104">Obsolete Types in the .NET Framework</span></span>

<a name="introduction"></a> <span data-ttu-id="1b42d-105">本文中的表格列出 .NET Framework 4.5 和 .NET Framework 4.6 中已淘汱類型 (依組件分組)。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="1b42d-105">The tables in this article list the types that are obsolete in the .NET Framework 4.5 and the .NET Framework 4.6, organized by assembly.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="1b42d-106">使用下列連結查看每個組件中過時的型別和建議的替代方案。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="1b42d-106">Use the following links to see a list of the obsolete types and the recommended alternatives in each assembly.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="1b42d-107">因為這些型別已經過時，其所有成員也已經過時。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="1b42d-107">Because these types are obsolete, all their members are also obsolete.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="1b42d-108">如需 .NET Framework 類別庫中其他過時成員的清單，請參閱[過時的成員](obsolete-members.md)。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="1b42d-108">For a list of additional obsolete members in the .NET Framework class library, see [Obsolete Members](obsolete-members.md).</span></span>

<a name="obsolete_types_in_system_assemblies"></a>

## <a name="obsolete-types-in-system-assemblies"></a><span data-ttu-id="1b42d-135">系統組件中的過時型別</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="1b42d-135">Obsolete Types in System Assemblies</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="1b42d-136">下列表格將列出已經在系統組件中宣告為過時的型別。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="1b42d-136">The following tables list the types that have been declared obsolete in system assemblies.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="1b42d-137">這些組件是用於以 .NET Framework 為目標的一般用途應用程式開發。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="1b42d-137">These assemblies are used for general\-purpose application development that targets the .NET Framework.</span></span>

<a name="obsolete_types_in_microsoft_assemblies"></a>

## <a name="obsolete-types-in-microsoft-assemblies"></a><span data-ttu-id="1b42d-926">Microsoft 組件中的過時型別</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="1b42d-926">Obsolete Types in Microsoft Assemblies</span></span>

<a name="IEHost"></a>

### <a name="assembly-iehostdll-and-ieexecexe"></a><span data-ttu-id="1b42d-929">組件：IEHost.dll 和 IEExec.exe</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="1b42d-929">Assembly: IEHost.dll and IEExec.exe</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="1b42d-930">IEHost.dll 和 IEExec.exe 組件已經從 .NET Framework 中移除。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="1b42d-930">The IEHost.dll and IEExec.exe assemblies have been removed from the .NET Framework.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="1b42d-931">其所有型別和成員都已淘汱，並自 .NET Framework 4 起不再支援。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="1b42d-931">All of their types and their members are obsolete and are not supported as of the .NET Framework 4.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="1b42d-932">這些組件之前是用來裝載 Windows Form 控制項以及在 Internet Explorer 中執行可執行檔。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="1b42d-932">These assemblies were used to host Windows Forms controls and to run executables in Internet Explorer.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="1b42d-933">建議的替代方案包括 ClickOnce、XAML 瀏覽器應用程式 (XBAP) 和 Microsoft Silverlight。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="1b42d-933">Recommended alternatives include ClickOnce, XAML browser applications (XBAP), and Microsoft Silverlight.</span></span>
